msg:I chose to travel during the last two days of the National Day. My friend recommended the Guangzhou Biquan Sky Hot Spring Hotel. This experience can be said to be very satisfactory and a bit beyond expectations.

Transportation location: Starting from Yuexiu Park in downtown Guangzhou, the journey will take one hour and 15 minutes if there is no traffic jam, and about one and a half hours if there is a traffic jam. The hotel has free underground parking with ample parking spaces.

Hotel environment: It is very new, the decoration is very new, the rooms are clean and tidy, the lobby, hot springs, locker rooms and other public environments are very good, not old at all, and well managed, and the cleaning is in place.

Service: The service is also very good. Check-in and check-out at the front desk are very fast. The waiters will take the initiative to say hello to the guests when they see them. They are quite enthusiastic. My room card was left in the restaurant, and a waiter immediately picked it up and handed it to the front desk of the restaurant. It was very Heartwarming.

Room: We booked a deluxe twin room, and the front desk upgraded us to a room with a swimming pool. The room is very large, with a balcony, a private pool, and separate toilets and showers. There is also a small imperial concubine couch, which the children like very much. Very satisfied with the room.

Hot spring area: It is on the third floor of the hotel. It can be reached directly by the elevator. It is very convenient. There is no need to change floors or transfer to other battery cars. You can just wear a swimsuit and come down. The hot spring area is not very big, and there are not many pools. Fortunately, there were not many people that day, and there were basically no people there. The pool water is relatively clean, and there are new towels and tea supplies nearby. There is also a place for children to play in the water.

Dinner: We ordered a dinner-inclusive buffet. The buffet was relatively average. There were only three types of seafood, shrimp, mussels, and white clams. The shrimp was a bit stale. Meats, no steaks, no chicken chops, no lamb chops, just barbecued meats, roasted pork and duck legs, Japanese food including salmon, conch slices, Spanish dace, tuna and sushi. Anyway, I think the buffet is just average. General. If you don‚Äôt want to eat at the hotel, there are many restaurants and food stalls outside for you to choose from.

Entertainment facilities: There are traditional Chinese massage and physiotherapy, a children's playground, a hot spring rest area, etc.

Generally speaking, the advantage of the hotel itself containing the hot spring area is that it is more convenient. It is directly accessible from the main building and there is no need to walk out. The slight drawback is that the hot spring area and pool are a bit small. It depends on personal needs. Anyway, my family of three thinks it is enough to have fun. I guess it will be a bit crowded if there are more people. The room is absolutely praiseworthy and satisfactory. The restaurant's food is mediocre, you can choose to eat outside, it's a hot spring hotel worth a second visit.

For eating, the buffet is on the second floor. We have breakfast. We have it at 7:30 in the morning. There are snacks, rice rolls, bread, porridge, etc. There are many options, and I personally feel that the ingredients are quite good. I haven't been to the hotel restaurant. There is Xingfu Building nearby, and Cantonese cuisine is delicious. There are also many farms, and I feel that Taojie‚Äôs products are delicious, but there are too many people on holidays.
The hot spring is on the third floor. I really like the clean water and hot springs. In summer, it is usually below 38 degrees. It is not too hot and children can also soak. There are also water slides, swimming pools, and bubble pools suitable for children. The children had a good time. The on-site service staff will warmly ask you if you want tea or water. The towels are very plentiful and praise. Soaked in the hot springs, ate dinner, and walked down the riverside of the hotel at night, which was very relaxing. To sum up, the hotel service staff are polite and professional, and they are very satisfied with the stay. It's worth coming a few more times.
